 Will they have to drink and eat for 20 hours a day or can there be a middle ground for their dilemma? Now according to Islamic hadith, in the Pak month of Ramadan, Allah has compelled the true Muslim to fast during the day and to pray at night
 lihaaja, norge or aasapaas ke kuch deshon main musalamaanon ko 20 ghante se adhik rojaa rakhana pad rahaa he or bache hue 2-3 ghante agle din ke roje kii taiyaari main lagaana pad rahaa he
 Actually, the date of Ramadan is determined from the lunar calendar, so every year this festival goes forward 11 days
 lihaaja beete 2 saal ke dauraan hi ramajaan kaa maheenaa garmi ke us samay par pahunch gaya he jab din ke mahaj 2-3 ghante ke liye yahaan suraj ast hota he

 isamen kisaanon ke khate main cash transfar, 5 lakh tak kii aay waalon ko tex main maafee ke saath-saath asangathit kshetra ke mazdooron ko pension sambandhi kai bade elaan kiye hai

 chidambaram ne is bajet ko vot kaa hisaab-kitaab bataaya he
 As per the customary practice in the country, the government completing the term presents the interim budget, and sometimes the vote on account is also presented in place of the interim budget
 chunki maujuuda sarkaar ke paas kaarykaal kaa kuch hi samay hota he, isliye navgathit sarkaar dwaara purna bajet pesh karne tak kaa kharch vahan karne ke liye sarkaar ko sansad se anumati leni hoti he
 Hence, no major announcements and policy decisions are usually taken by the government in such a budget
 isliye isamen maatr kuch maheenon ke aay or vyay kaa byora bhar hota he
 Because the present government cannot impose its financial decisions on the incoming government
 haalanki antarim bajet naam kaa koi shabd samvidhan main maujuud nahin he, lihaaja yah bas ek swasthy loktantric parampara kaa hissaa bhar he
 But in this budget, the Modi government at the center announced an exemption from tax on income up to 5 lakh, direct cash transfer to the account of small and marginal farmers

 jiske tahat 100 rupee pratimah premium ke bhugtan par 60 saal kii aayu ke baad unhen 3000 rupee pratimah pension dene kaa elaan kiya gaya he
 These are all such schemes, which will bear the burden of the incoming government
 loksabhaa chunaav ke baad jo nai sarkaar banegi niyamat: use hi purna bajet pesh karne kaa adhikaar hota he
 But the stakes that the Modi government has played by making such big announcements in its interim budget will have to be stretched even bigger by the incoming government to reverse it
 masalan 5 lakh tak kii aay ko tex ke daayre se baahar rakhane kaa faisla madhyam varg ke liye badi raahat kii khabar he

 unhone bataaya ki shuruaati jaankaree ke mutabik kareeb 52 varshiya ali bhartiya sena kii jasusi karke iesai ko mahatvapurn suchanaaen detaa tha
 He married in Pakistan and the father of two children used to visit Pakistan often on the pretext of meeting his family
 isi dauraan vah iesai ke sampark main aayaa tha
 Goyal said that Ali's capture important documents of the Indian Army, ATM cards of one Pakistani and two Indian banks, two passbooks and checkbooks, a check of eight thousand rupees from Pakistan Bank Al Habib, three mobile phones, two datacards, Six SIM cards, passports and mini laptop receipts have been recovered
 yah raseed us laptop kii he, jise jhaansi ke babina kaint main ek faujee ke bete ko kharidkar diya gaya he
 He said that Ali has admitted during interrogation that he had met an ISI officer named Zahid seven-eight years ago, since then he has been sending information about the Indian Army to the Pakistani intelligence agency
 saudi arab main naukariyaan chale jane ke baad gambhir aarthik sankat se hajaaron bhartiya kamgaaron ke jujhane ke bich videsh rajyamantri ve
 K
 singh sthiti kaa jayja lene or swadesh lautne ko icchhuk logon ko waapas laane ke taur tareekon ko antim rup dene ke liye mangalvaar raat khadi desh ke liye ravaanaa hue
 Prior to VK Singh's visit, the Indian embassy in New Delhi started an initiative to collect details of Indian workers laid off by employers
 philhal, kul 7,700 prabhavit bhartiya kaamgaar 20 shiviron main rah rahe hai
 The embassy is collecting details about other Indian workers living in different parts of Saudi Arabia
 wike singh mangalvaar raat dubai ke raste jeddah ke liye ravaanaa hue
 Foreign Ministry spokesman Vikas Swaroop said that their assessment at the ground level would decide the course of action
 kachche tel kii keemten ghatane or saudi arab kii sarkaar dwaara kharchon main katautee karne ke kaaran is khadi desh kii arthvyavastha mandi kii shikaar ho gai he, jisase hajaaron bharatiyon kii naukari chali gai he
 The Indian Mission has provided food to those unable to buy food
 mangalvaar ko isse pehle, khadi deshon se jude maamalon ko dekhne vaale wike singh ke mantrimandal sahyogi em
 J
 akbar ne bharat main saudi arab ke rajdoot saud bin mohammad al saati se mulaakaat kar berozegaar bharatiyon kii sthiti par charchaa kii
 Akbar tweeted, 'saudi Ambassador to India Dr
 saud bin mohammad al saati se sabhi dwipaksheeya muddon par sakaaratmak charchaa hui
 i am happy to receive assurances and support from the Saudi government towards resolving all issues, including Indian workers
 ' External Affairs Minister Sushma Swaraj said on Monday that all affected Indian workers would be brought back
 bhartiya duutavas se ek team ne kamgaaron ke kanoonee bakaayon ke sangrakshan se judi prakriya puri karne ke liye somvaar ko saudi arab ke shram adhikariyon se mulaakaat kii thi
 Swaroop said that the Indian embassy in Riyadh held a meeting of community social workers on Monday, in which the ambassador sought their help in gathering information about the affected workers
 unhen ek prapatr uplabdh karaayaa gaya, jis par maang soochna is duutavas ko saunpi jaani he
 The government has also requested Saudi Arabian authorities to grant withdrawal visas to unemployed Indian workers without an NOC of employers, and also to settle the arrears of employees who have had salaries for several months
 videsh mantralay ke adhikariyon ne bataaya ki wike singh buudhvaar tadake jedda pahunch jaaenge or shuukravaar kii shaam tak unke lautne kaa kaarykram he
 He is going to Jeddah via Dubai
 swaroop ne bataaya ki messors saudi ogar se jude 4,072 bhartiya kaamgaar riyaad main nau shiviron main rah rahe hai, vahiin messors saad group se jude 1,457 karmchaariyon ko dammam main do shiviron main rakhaa gaya he
 Five workers from m / s Shifa Sanaya are in a camp in Riyadh, while 13 Indian employees of m / s Tayya Contracting Company are staying in a camp
 swaroop ne bataaya ki riyaad main chaudaa shiviron main rah rahe kul 5,547 bhartiya kamgaaron ko bhartiya duutavas dwaara sahaayta uplabdh karai ja rahi he
 Swarup said, 'apart from these, there are 2,153 Indian workers attached to Messrs Saudi Ogar in six camps in Jeddah who have been provided food by the Indian Consulate
 is tarah se kul 7,700 prabhavit bhartiya kaamgaar 20 shiviron main hai
 The embassy teams went to six camps in Riyadh on Monday
 videsh mantralay ke pravaktaa ne kaha, 'prayek kaamgaar, uski kul seva, bakaayaa vetan, baahar nikalne
 Remained in the job
 sthanantaran kii ichha ke bare main alag-alag soochna ikattha kii ja rahi he
 Foreign Minister Sushma Swaraj had said in Parliament on Monday that the workers would be brought back to India
 unhone jor dekar kaha tha ki unamem se kisi ko bhi bhookha nahin rahanaa hoga
 The comments swaraj ne kaha ki bharat sarkaar saudi arab ke videsh or shramik vibhaag ke sampark main he
 He said that the affected Indians would be evacuated as soon as possible
 (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) wike singh kii yatra se pehle nai dilli main bhartiya duutavas ne niyoktaaon dwaara chantni kar die bhartiya kamgaaron kaa vivaran jutaney kii pahal shuru kii he
 Currently, a total of 7,700 affected Indian workers are living in 20 camps
 duutavas saudi arab ke vibhinn hisson main rah rahe anya bhartiya kamgaaron ke bare main vivaran juta rahaa he
 VK Singh left for Jeddah via Dubai on Tuesday night
 videsh mantralay ke pravaktaa vikaas swaroop ne kaha ki jamini str par unka akalan aage kii karrwai tay karegaa
 The economy of this Gulf country has fallen victim to the recession due to falling crude oil prices and the Saudi Arabian government's spending cuts, leaving thousands of Indians jobless

 swaroop ne bataaya ki riyaad main bhartiya duutavas ne saamudayik saamaajik kaaryakartaaon kii somvaar ko ek baithak kii, jisamen rajdoot ne prabhavit kamgaaron ke bare main suchanaaen jutaney main unki madad maangi thi
 They were provided with a form, on which demand information is to be submitted to this embassy
 sarkaar ne saudi arab ke adhikariyon se niyoktaaon ke enosi ke bagaiyr berozegaar bhartiya kamgaaron ko nikasi vija dene kaa anurodh kiya he or un karmchaariyon ke bakaae kaa niptaan karne kaa bhi anurodh kiya he jin karmchaariyon ke kai maheenon se vetan bakaayaa hai
 Foreign Ministry officials said that VK Singh would reach Jeddah in the early hours of Wednesday and was scheduled to return by Friday evening
 vah dubai hokar jedda ja rahe hai
 Swaroop said that 4,072 Indian workers belonging to Messrs Saudi Ogar are living in nine camps in Riyadh, while 1,457 employees belonging to Messrs Saad Group have been placed in two camps in Dammam
 macers shipha sanaaya ke paanch kaamgaar riyaad main ek shivi main hai, jabaki macers taiyaa contrecting company ke 13 bhartiya karmchaaree ek shivi main tehre hue hai
 Swaroop said that a total of 5,547 Indian workers living in fourteen camps in Riyadh are being assisted by the Indian Embassy
 swaroop ne kaha, 'inke alaava, jeddah main chah shiviron main messors saudi ogar se jude 2,153 bhartiya kaamgaar hai jinhen bhartiya vaanijya duutavas dwaara bhojan uplabdh karaayaa gaya he

 naukari main bane rahe
